                  Turbulent air.
                </label>

      <div class="text-center section-header" id="faa_header">
        <h1>Questions 1&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;5</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>Which technique should a pilot use to scan for traffic?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="true">
                  Systematically focus on different segments of the sky for short intervals.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="false">
                  Continuous sweeping of the windshield from right to left.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="false">
                  Concentrate on relative movement detected in the peripheral vision area.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to figure 25, area 2.) The floor of Class B airspace at Addison Airport is</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_25/main-57bc6a20997504c7dfe6d1e894e7811561453c502faadd4248a5f29a8ea0c65e.png">Figure 25</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_25/area2-075d3f95fa650447df66f4db7be9a4f3ff0cb980b777463f18740610123dd856.png">Figure 25 - Area2</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="false">
                  3,000 feet MSL
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="false">
                  at the surface
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="true">
                  2,500 feet MSL
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>When requesting a waiver, the required documents should be presented to the FAA at least how many days prior to the planned operation?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_0" value="false">
                  10 days
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_1" value="false">
                  30 days
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_2" value="true">
                  90 days
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>Which technique should a remote pilot use to scan for traffic? A remote pilot should</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_0" value="false">
                  concentrate on relative movement detected in the peripheral vision area.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_1" value="true">
                  systematically focus on different segments of the sky for short intervals.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_2" value="false">
                  continuously scan the sky from right to left.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>Responsibility for collision avoidance in controlled airspace rests with</h3>

      <div class="text-center section-header" id="faa_header">
        <h1>Questions 1&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;5</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>What is the antidote when a pilot has a hazardous attitude, such as Invulnerability?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="true">
                  It could happen to me
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="false">
                  It can not be that bad
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="false">
                  It will not happen to me
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>What is the antidote when a pilot has a hazardous attitude, such as Resignation?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="true">
                  I am not helpless
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="false">
                  What is the use
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="false">
                  Someone else is responsible
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to figure 22, area 1.) Th floor of the controlled airspace overlying the Sandpoint Airport is</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_22/main-59e73d0ce68fcab9527e721d776f74bd35c9783517ac70e9fbc530d2f7b584a7.png">Figure 22</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_0" value="false">
                  700 feet MSL
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_1" value="true">
                  700 feet AGL
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_2" value="false">
                  at the surface
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>If an unstable air mass is forced upward, what type clouds can be expected?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_0" value="false">
                  Stratus clouds with considerable associated turbulence.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_1" value="false">
                  Stratus clouds with little vertical development.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_2" value="true">
                  Clouds with considerable vertical development and associated turbulence.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>According to 14 CFR part 48, when must a person register a small UA with the Federal Aviation Administration?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_0" value="false">
                  When the small UA is used for any purpose other than as a model aircraft.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_1" value="false">
                  Only when the operator will be paid for commercial services.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_2" value="true">
                  All civilian small UAs weighing greater than .55 pounds must be registered regardless of its intended use.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>

        <h1>Questions 1&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;5</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>What are characteristics of a moist, unstable air mass?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="false">
                  Poor visibility and smooth air.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="false">
                  Stratiform clouds and showery precipitation.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="true">
                  Cumuliform clouds and showery precipitation.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>When operating near an uncontrolled airport, which frequency should the remote-pilot use to monitor air traffic?</h3>

                </label>
              </div>

                </label>

                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="false">
                  AWOS
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>Which technique should a pilot use to scan for traffic?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_0" value="false">
                  Concentrate on relative movement detected in the peripheral vision area.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_1" value="true">

                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_2" value="false">

                </label>
              </div>
          </div>

    <div class="col-sm-9">
      <div class="text-center section-header" id="faa_header">
        <h1>Questions 1&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;5</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to figure 20 area 4.) What hazards to aircraft may exist in restricted areas such as R-5302B?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_20/main-7bb39947fef2e22d315ec0cc555cad991fa39b6782cfd7875796894340f3ae68.png">Figure 20</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="true">
                  Unusual, often invisible, hazards such as aerial gunnery or guided missiles.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="false">
                  Military training activities that necessitate acrobatic or abrupt flight maneuvers.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="false">
                  High volume of pilot training or an unusual type of aerial activity.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to Figure 21.) You have been hired by a farmer to use your small UA to inspect his crops. The area that you are to survey is in the Devil`s Lake West MOA, east of area 2. How would you find out if the MOA is active?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_21/main-310f135d42123ac9656452743e4d40276598dbb31a45d091f472d322dadc7f36.png">Figure 21</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="true">
                  Contact Flight Service
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="false">
                  Refer to the Military Operations Directory.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="false">
                  Locate the information in the Small UAS database.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>When operating an unmanned airplane, the remote pilot should consider that the load factor on the wings may be increased anytime</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_0" value="true">
                  the airplane is subjected to maneuvers other than straight and level flight.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_1" value="false">
                  the CG is shifted rearward to the aft CG limit.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_2" value="false">
                  the gross weight is reduced.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to Figure 22, area 2.) At Coeur D’Alene which frequency should be used as a Common Traffic Advisory Frequency (CTAF) to monitor airport traffic?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_22/main-59e73d0ce68fcab9527e721d776f74bd35c9783517ac70e9fbc530d2f7b584a7.png">Figure 22</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_22/area_2-e763a0c6d57e61f8766e0f5059568618a209db497ca1629e5f97f96336d77bee.png">Figure 22 - Area 2</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_0" value="false">
                  122.05 MHz.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_1" value="true">
                  122.8 MHz.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_2" value="false">
                  135.075 MHz.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>You are a remote pilot for a co-op energy service provider. You are to use your UA to inspect power lines in a remote area 15 hours away from your home office. After the drive, fatigue impacts your abilities to complete your assignment on time. Fatigue can be recognized</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_0" value="false">
                  by an ability to overcome sleep deprivation.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_1" value="true">
                  as being in an impaired state.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_2" value="false">
                  easily by an experienced pilot.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
        <div class="row">
          <div class="col-sm-8 col-sm-offset-2">
            <button type="submit" id="faa_submit" class="btn btn-primary btn-lg btn-block">Grade my responses</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </form>
    </div>

              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_26/main-23f81c5aa1fa0a31c0bc01f38eda96971578c77425a661434cb9515d4782e96a.png">Figure 26</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="false">
                  The degrees of latitude east and west of the line that passes through Greenwich, England.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="false">
                  The degrees of latitude east and west of the Prime Meridian.
                </label>
              </div>

            <h3>(Refer to figure 15)  What is the forecast wind for KMEM from 1600Z until the end of the forecast?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_15/main-9a47406eb4502bdf2bf63d153970e04c9c9375c955f1fc5f54031e38e2395bad.png">Figure 15</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="false">
                  No significant wind.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="false">
                  Variable in direction at 4 knots.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="true">
                  Variable in direction at 6 knots.
                </label>
              </div>

                  the controlling agency
                </label>
              </div>

                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="true">

                </label>

                </label>

              <div class="radio">

                  Terminal Area Chart (TAC).
                </label>

                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_1" value="true">

        <h1>Questions 1&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;5</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to Figure 20.) How would a remote PIC &quot;CHECK NOTAMS&quot; as noted in the CAUTION box regarding the unmarked balloon?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_20/main-7bb39947fef2e22d315ec0cc555cad991fa39b6782cfd7875796894340f3ae68.png">Figure 20</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="true">
                  By obtaining a briefing via an online source such as 1800WXBrief.com.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="false">
                  By utilizing the B4UFLY mobile application.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="false">
                  By contacting the FAA district office.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>What is a characteristic of stable air?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="false">
                  Cumulus clouds
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="false">
                  Unlimited visibility
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="true">
                  Stratiform clouds
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to figure 15) In the TAF from KOKC, the clear sky becomes</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_15/main-9a47406eb4502bdf2bf63d153970e04c9c9375c955f1fc5f54031e38e2395bad.png">Figure 15</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_0" value="false">
                  overcast at 200 feet with the probability of becoming overcast at 400 feet during the forecast period between 2200Z and 2400Z.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_1" value="false">
                  overcast at 200 feet with a 40% probability of becoming overcast at 600 feet during the forecast period between 2200Z and 2400Z.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_2" value="true">
                  overcast at 2,000 feet during the forecast period between 2200Z and 2400Z.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>What is the purpose of the rudder on an airplane?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_0" value="true">
                  To control yaw
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_1" value="false">
                  To control roll
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_2" value="false">
                  To control overbanking tendency
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>When loading cameras or other equipment on an sUAS, mount the items in a manner that</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_0" value="false">
                  Is visible to the visual observer or other crewmembers.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_1" value="false">
                  Can be easily removed without the use of tools.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_2" value="true">
                  Does not adversly affect the center of gravity.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
        <div class="row">
          <div class="col-sm-8 col-sm-offset-2">
            <button type="submit" id="faa_submit" class="btn btn-primary btn-lg btn-block">Grade my responses</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </form>

            <li><a class="btn-sm" href="/faa/drone-practice-tests/17/">Questions 81&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;85</a></li>
            <li><a class="btn-sm" href="/faa/drone-practice-tests/18/">Questions 86&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;90</a></li>
            <li><a class="btn-sm" href="/faa/drone-practice-tests/19/">Questions 91&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;95</a></li>
            <li><a class="btn-sm" href="/faa/drone-practice-tests/20/">Questions 96&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;100</a></li>
            <li><a class="btn-sm" href="/faa/drone-practice-tests/21/">Questions 101&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;105</a></li>
            <li><a class="btn-sm" href="/faa/drone-practice-tests/22/">Questions 106&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;110</a></li>
            <li><a class="btn-sm" href="/faa/drone-practice-tests/23/">Questions 111&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;115</a></li>
            <li><a class="btn-sm" href="/faa/drone-practice-tests/24/">Questions 116&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;120</a></li>
            <li><a class="btn-sm" href="/faa/drone-practice-tests/25/">Questions 121&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;125</a></li>
            <li><a class="btn-sm" href="/faa/drone-practice-tests/26/">Question 126</a></li>
        </ul>
      </nav>
    </div>
    <div class="col-sm-9">
      <div class="text-center section-header" id="faa_header">
        <h1>Questions 1&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;5</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>While operating a small unmanned aircraft system (sUAS), you experience a flyaway and several people suffer injuries. Which of the following injuries requires reporting to the FAA?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="true">
                  An injury requiring a hospitalization over 48 hours
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="false">
                  Minor bruises
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="false">
                  Scrapes and cuts bandaged on site
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>A person whose sole task is watching the sUAS to report hazards to the rest of the crew is called</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="false">
                  Person manipulating the controls
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="false">
                  Remote-PIC
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="true">
                  Visual observer
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to figure 2.) If an airplane weighs 23 pounds, what approximate weight would the airplane structure be required to support during a 60° banked turn while maintaining altitude?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_2/main-08aec798e611ae97212586f5e0fb9366d877818523df8aaba1a75f1c8597b872.png">Figure 2</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_0" value="true">
                  46 pounds
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_1" value="false">
                  23 pounds
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_2" value="false">
                  34 pounds
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>When loading cameras or other equipment on an sUAS, mount the items in a manner that</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_0" value="false">
                  Can be easily removed without the use of tools.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_1" value="false">
                  Is visible to the visual observer or other crewmembers.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_2" value="true">
                  Does not adversly affect the center of gravity.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>What are characteristics of a moist, unstable air mass?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_0" value="true">
                  Turbulence and showery precipitation.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_1" value="false">
                  Poor visibility and smooth air.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_2" value="false">
                  Haze and smoke.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
        <div class="row">
          <div class="col-sm-8 col-sm-offset-2">
            <button type="submit" id="faa_submit" class="btn btn-primary btn-lg btn-block">Grade my responses</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </form>
    </div>

    <div class="col-sm-9">
      <div class="text-center section-header" id="faa_header">
        <h1>Questions 1&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;5</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>If an unstable air mass is forced upward, what type clouds can be expected?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="false">
                  Stratus clouds with considerable associated turbulence.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="false">
                  Stratus clouds with little vertical development.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="true">
                  Clouds with considerable vertical development and associated turbulence.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>Which crewmember is required to be under the direct supervision of the Remote PIC when operating an sUAS?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="true">
                  The person manipulating the controls
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="false">
                  The Remote Pilot in Command (Remote PIC)
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="false">
                  The visual observer (VO)
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>When loading cameras or other equipment on an sUAS, mount the items in a manner that</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_0" value="false">
                  Is visible to the visual observer or other crewmembers.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_1" value="false">
                  Can be easily removed without the use of tools.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_2" value="true">
                  Does not adversly affect the center of gravity.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>When adapting crew resource management (CRM) concepts to the operation of a small UA, CRM must be integrated into</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_0" value="false">
                  the flight portion only.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_1" value="true">
                  all phases of the operation.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_2" value="false">
                  the communications only.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>Under what condition would a small UAS not have to be registered before it is operated in the United States?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_0" value="false">
                  All small UAS need to be registered regardless of the weight of the aircraft before, during, or after the flight.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_1" value="false">
                  When the aircraft has a takeoff weight that is more than .55 pounds, but less than 55 pounds, not including fuel and necessary attachments.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_2" value="true">
                  When the aircraft weighs less than .55 pounds on takeoff, including everything that is on-board or attached to the aircraft.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
        <div class="row">
          <div class="col-sm-8 col-sm-offset-2">
            <button type="submit" id="faa_submit" class="btn btn-primary btn-lg btn-block">Grade my responses</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </form>
    </div>

    <div class="col-sm-9">
      <div class="text-center section-header" id="faa_header">
        <h1>Questions 1&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;5</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>What should pilots state initially when telephoning a weather briefing facility for preflight weather information?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="false">
                  the remote-PIC certificate number
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="true">
                  the location of the sUA operation
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="false">
                  the address of the remote-PIC
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>What could be a consequence of operating a small unmanned aircraft above its maximum allowable weight?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="true">
                  Shorter endurance
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="false">
                  Faster speed
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="false">
                  Increased maneuverability
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>According to 14 CFR part 107, how may a remote pilot operate an unmanned aircraft in class C airspace?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_0" value="false">
                  The remote pilot must monitor the Air Traffic Control (ATC) frequency from launch to recovery.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_1" value="false">
                  The remote pilot must contact the Air Traffic Control (ATC) facility after launching the unmanned aircraft.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_2" value="true">
                  The remote pilot must have prior authorization from the Air Traffic Control (ATC) facility having jurisdiction over that airspace.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>Under what condition would a small UAS not have to be registered before it is operated in the United States?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_0" value="true">
                  When the aircraft weighs less than .55 pounds on takeoff, including everything that is on-board or attached to the aircraft.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_1" value="false">
                  All small UAS need to be registered regardless of the weight of the aircraft before, during, or after the flight.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_2" value="false">
                  When the aircraft has a takeoff weight that is more than .55 pounds, but less than 55 pounds, not including fuel and necessary attachments.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to figure 25, area 7.) The airspace overlying Mc Kinney airport (TKI) is controlled from the surface to</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_25/main-57bc6a20997504c7dfe6d1e894e7811561453c502faadd4248a5f29a8ea0c65e.png">Figure 25</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_0" value="true">
                  2,900 feet MSL
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_1" value="false">
                  700 feet AGL
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_2" value="false">
                  2,500 feet MSL
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>

      <div class="text-center section-header" id="faa_header">
        <h1>Questions 1&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;5</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to figure 15) In the TAF from KOKC, the clear sky becomes</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_15/main-9a47406eb4502bdf2bf63d153970e04c9c9375c955f1fc5f54031e38e2395bad.png">Figure 15</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="false">
                  overcast at 200 feet with the probability of becoming overcast at 400 feet during the forecast period between 2200Z and 2400Z.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="true">
                  overcast at 2,000 feet during the forecast period between 2200Z and 2400Z.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="false">
                  overcast at 200 feet with a 40% probability of becoming overcast at 600 feet during the forecast period between 2200Z and 2400Z.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to figure 22, area 1.) The elevation of the Shoshone County Airport is</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_22/main-59e73d0ce68fcab9527e721d776f74bd35c9783517ac70e9fbc530d2f7b584a7.png">Figure 22</a></li>

      <div class="text-center section-header" id="faa_header">
        <h1>Questions 1&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;5</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>You have been hired as a remote pilot by a local TV news station to film breaking news with a small UA. You expressed a safety concern and the station manager has instructed you to “fly first, ask questions later.” What type of attitude does this attitude represent?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="true">
                  Impulsivity.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="false">
                  Invulnerability.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="false">
                  Machismo.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>A pilot should be able to overcome the symptoms or avoid future occurrences of hyperventilation by</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="true">
                  slowing the breathing rate, breathing into a bag, or talking aloud.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="false">
                  increasing the breathing rate in order to increase lung ventilation.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="false">
                  closely monitoring the aircraft&#39;s telemetry data.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to Figure 20.) Who would a Remote Pilot in Command contact to &quot;CHECK NOTAMS&quot; as it is noted in the CAUTION box regarding the unmarked balloon?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_20/main-7bb39947fef2e22d315ec0cc555cad991fa39b6782cfd7875796894340f3ae68.png">Figure 20</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_0" value="true">
                  Flight Service
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_1" value="false">
                  NTSB office
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_2" value="false">
                  FAA district office
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>Which factor would tend to increase the density altitude at a given airport?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_0" value="false">
                  A decrease in relative humidity
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_1" value="true">
                  An increase in ambient temperature
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_2" value="false">
                  An increase in barometric pressure
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to figure 2.) If an airplane weighs 33 pounds, what approximate weight would the airplane structure be required to support during a 30° banked turn while maintaining altitude?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_2/main-08aec798e611ae97212586f5e0fb9366d877818523df8aaba1a75f1c8597b872.png">Figure 2</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_0" value="false">
                  31 pounds
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_1" value="false">
                  12 pounds
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_2" value="true">
                  40 pounds
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>

      <div class="text-center section-header" id="faa_header">
        <h1>Questions 1&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;5</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>What should pilots state initially when telephoning a weather briefing facility for preflight weather information?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="false">
                  the address of the remote-PIC
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="false">
                  the remote-PIC certificate number
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="true">
                  the location of the sUA operation
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>While operating a small unmanned aircraft system (sUAS), you experience a flyaway and several people suffer injuries. Which of the following injuries requires reporting to the FAA?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="false">
                  Minor bruises
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="false">
                  Scrapes and cuts bandaged on site
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="true">
                  An injury requiring a hospitalization over 48 hours
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>According to 14 CFR part 48, when must a person register a small UA with the Federal Aviation Administration?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_0" value="false">
                  Only when the operator will be paid for commercial services.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_1" value="true">
                  All civilian small UAs weighing greater than .55 pounds must be registered regardless of its intended use.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_2" value="false">
                  When the small UA is used for any purpose other than as a model aircraft.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>What is the antidote when a pilot has a hazardous attitude, such as Resignation?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_0" value="false">
                  Someone else is responsible
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_1" value="false">
                  What is the use
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_2" value="true">
                  I am not helpless
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>According to 14 CFR part 107, who is responsible for determining the performance of a small unmanned aircraft?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_0" value="false">
                  Manufacturer.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_1" value="true">
                  Remote pilot-in-command.
                </label>

                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_2" value="false">
                  Owner or operator.

    <div class="col-sm-9">
      <div class="text-center section-header" id="faa_header">
        <h1>Questions 1&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;5</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>Within how many days must an sUAS accident be reported to the FAA?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="false">
                  90 days
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="true">
                  10 days
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="false">
                  30 days
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>A local TV station has hired a remote pilot to operate their small UA to cover breaking news stories. The remote pilot has had multiple near misses with obstacles on the ground and two small UAS accidents. What would be a solution for the news station to improve their operating safety culture?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="false">
                  The news station should implement a policy of no more than five crashes/incidents within 6 months.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="true">
                  The news station should recognize hazardous attitudes and situations and develop standard operating procedures that emphasize safety.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="false">
                  The news station does not need to make any changes; there are times that an accident is unavoidable.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>A pilot should be able to overcome the symptoms or avoid future occurrences of hyperventilation by</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_0" value="false">
                  closely monitoring the aircraft&#39;s telemetry data.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_1" value="false">
                  increasing the breathing rate in order to increase lung ventilation.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_2" value="true">
                  slowing the breathing rate, breathing into a bag, or talking aloud.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to Figure 21.) What airport is located approximately 47 (degrees) 40 (minutes) N latitude and 101 (degrees) 26 (minutes) W longitude?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_21/main-310f135d42123ac9656452743e4d40276598dbb31a45d091f472d322dadc7f36.png">Figure 21</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_0" value="false">
                  Mercer County Regional Airport.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_1" value="false">
                  Semshenko Airport.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_2" value="true">
                  Garrison Airport.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>A stable air mass is most likely to have which characteristics?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_0" value="false">
                  Turbulent air.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_1" value="false">
                  Showery precipitation.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_2" value="true">
                  Poor surface visibility.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>

    <div class="col-sm-9">
      <div class="text-center section-header" id="faa_header">
        <h1>Questions 1&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;5</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>When adapting crew resource management (CRM) concepts to the operation of a small UA, CRM must be integrated into</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="false">
                  the communications only.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="true">
                  all phases of the operation.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="false">
                  the flight portion only.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to Figure 21, area 2.) What is the floor of controlled airspace along V15?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_21/main-310f135d42123ac9656452743e4d40276598dbb31a45d091f472d322dadc7f36.png">Figure 21</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_21/area_2-f6dcdf188614931df67f59b71f4ad4a05b0839255d29c45f3c25813450e308ed.png">Figure 21 - Area 2</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="false">
                  14,500 ft MSL
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="true">
                  1200 ft AGL
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="false">
                  Refer to the Chart Supplements
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to Figure 20.) Why would the small flag at Lake Drummond in area 2 of the sectional chart be important to a Remote PIC?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_20/main-7bb39947fef2e22d315ec0cc555cad991fa39b6782cfd7875796894340f3ae68.png">Figure 20</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_0" value="false">
                  The flag indicates that there will be a large obstruction depicted on the next printing of the chart.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_1" value="false">
                  The flag indicates a GPS check point that can be used by both manned and remote pilots for orientation.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_2" value="true">
                  The flag indicates a VFR check point for manned aircraft, and a higher volume of air traffic should be expected there.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>To get a complete weather overview for the planned flight, the Remote Pilot in Command should obtain a</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_0" value="false">
                  An abbreviated briefing
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_1" value="true">
                  A standard briefing
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_2" value="false">
                  An outlook briefing
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>During your preflight inspection, you discover a small nick in the casing of your sUAS battery. What action should you take?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_0" value="true">
                  Follow the manufacturer&#39;s guidance.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_1" value="false">
                  Throw it away with your household trash.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_2" value="false">
                  Use it as long as it will still hold a charge.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
        <div class="row">
          <div class="col-sm-8 col-sm-offset-2">
            <button type="submit" id="faa_submit" class="btn btn-primary btn-lg btn-block">Grade my responses</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </form>

      <div class="text-center section-header" id="faa_header">
        <h1>Questions 1&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;5</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>You may operate an sUAS from a moving vehicle when no property is carried for compensation or hire</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="false">
                  Over suburban areas
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="false">
                  Over a parade or other social events
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="true">
                  Over a sparsely populated area
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to figure 25, area 4.) The floor of Class B airspace overlying Hicks Airport (T67) north-northwest of Fort Worth Meacham Field is</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_25/main-57bc6a20997504c7dfe6d1e894e7811561453c502faadd4248a5f29a8ea0c65e.png">Figure 25</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="true">
                  4,000 feet MSL
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="false">
                  3,200 feet MSL
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="false">
                  at the surface
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to Figure 20, area 6) What does the dashed magenta line East of Area 6 indicate?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_20/main-7bb39947fef2e22d315ec0cc555cad991fa39b6782cfd7875796894340f3ae68.png">Figure 20</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">

                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
